### [56] [HI Content of Group Galaxies from the FAST All Sky HI Survey](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.22902)
*Shulan Yan,Andrew Ma,Qingzheng Yu,Taotao Fang,Chuan He,Ming Zhu*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 利用FAST的盲测数据，研究了星系群中原子氢（HI）含量，发现HI耗尽主要局限于卫星星系和致密核心区域，而非整个星系群普遍存在。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究星系群中星系的原子气体含量是否与孤立星系不同，以理解环境对星系演化的影响。

Method: 基于FAST全天天文HI巡天的早期数据，构建包含230个星系群成员星系及匹配的孤立星系对照样本，采用删失数据建模方法分析HI含量（包括探测与未探测结果）。

Result: 在恒星质量和颜色固定的情况下，星系群整体HI分数中位数与对照组差异仅为-0.04 dex（95%置信区间[-0.18, 0.16]）；但存在内部差异：卫星星系HI贫乏（Δf_HI = -0.12 dex），中心星系则接近正常或轻微富集（Δf_HI = +0.13 dex）；位于R<0.5R₁₈₀或高密度环境（丰富度>10或局部密度>10 gal Mpc⁻²）的星系HI耗尽可能更强，而外围星系与对照组无显著差异。

Conclusion: HI耗尽并非普遍存在于所有星系群成员中，而是主要集中于卫星星系和致密核心区域，表明环境效应在小尺度结构中更为显著。

Abstract: We investigate the atomic gas (HI) content of galaxies in groups using early
data from the FAST All Sky HI survey (FASHI). Taking advantage of FAST's blind,
wide-area coverage and uniform sensitivity, we assemble a sample of $230$ group
galaxies and a matched control sample of isolated systems, and apply
censored-data modeling to include both detections and non-detections. At fixed
stellar mass and color, we find that the global median HI fraction of group
galaxies differs from that of controls by only $-0.04$ dex ($95\%$ CI [$-0.18,\
0.16$]), indicating at most a mild average offset. The signal is not uniform
across populations: satellites are HI-poor (median $\Delta
f_{\mathrm{HI}}=-0.12$ dex), whereas centrals are consistent with normal to
mildly HI-rich (median $\Delta f_{\mathrm{HI}}=0.13$ dex). Group galaxies
located within $0.5R_{180}$ and in denser systems (richness $>10$ or local
density $\Sigma>10\ \mathrm{gal\ Mpc^{-2}}$) show stronger negative offsets,
whereas galaxies in the outskirts are statistically indistinguishable from the
controls. These results refine earlier reports of global group HI deficiency:
with deeper blind data and uniform treatment of upper limits, we show that HI
depletion is primarily confined to satellites and compact cores rather than
being ubiquitous across groups.

</details>


### [57] [Revisiting the 150 MHz Radio Luminosity Function of Star-Forming Galaxies with LOFAR Deep Fields through a Refined Statistical Framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.22934)
*Wenjie Wang,Zunli Yuan,Hongwei Yu,Yang Liu,Yu Luo,Puxun Wu*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本研究利用LOFAR巡天数据，结合核密度估计与参数建模，分析了0 < z < 5.7星系的150 MHz射电光度函数，发现联合光度与密度演化（LADE）模型显著优于纯光度演化模型，揭示了恒星形成星系射电辐射的演化规律。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解恒星形成星系在宇宙时间中的射电辐射演化，需准确刻画其光度函数的红移演化行为，传统方法受限于分箱和参数假设，因此需要更灵活且稳健的方法。

Method: 采用自适应核密度估计（KDE）无参数重建光度函数，并结合最大似然法拟合纯光度演化（PLE）和两种联合光度密度演化（LADE）模型，考虑完备性校正及本地射电光度函数和源计数约束。

Result: KDE揭示了明显的联合光度与密度演化特征；信息准则强烈支持LADE优于PLE；LADE模型能一致地再现观测到的光度函数和源计数，而PLE表现较差；在亮端发现轻微超出，可能源于AGN污染残留。

Conclusion: 联合光度与密度演化是描述恒星形成星系射电光度函数演化的更优框架，结合非参数与参数方法可为未来SKA等巡天提供可靠分析范式。

Abstract: We present a comprehensive analysis of the 150~MHz radio luminosity function
(LF) of star-forming galaxies (SFGs) using deep observations from the LOFAR
Two-metre Sky Survey in the ELAIS-N1, Bo\"{o}tes, and Lockman Hole fields. Our
sample comprises $\sim$56,000 SFGs over $0 < z < 5.7$. We first analyze the
deepest field (ELAIS-N1), then jointly model all three fields while accounting
for their distinct flux limits and selection functions. Using adaptive kernel
density estimation (KDE), we reconstruct the LF continuously across redshift
and luminosity without binning or parametric assumptions. The KDE results
reveal clear signatures of joint luminosity and density evolution (LADE).
Motivated by this, we construct and fit three parametric models--pure
luminosity evolution (PLE) and two LADE variants--using a full
maximum-likelihood method that includes completeness corrections and
constraints from the local radio LF and Euclidean-normalized source counts
(SCs). Model selection using Akaike and Bayesian Information Criteria strongly
favors LADE over PLE. For ELAIS-N1, the more flexible LADE model (Model C)
provides the best fit, while for the combined fields, the simpler Model B
balances fit quality and complexity more effectively. Both LADE models
reproduce the observed LFs and SCs across luminosity and flux density ranges,
whereas PLE underperforms. We also identify a mild excess at the bright end of
the LF, likely due to residual AGN contamination. This study demonstrates that
combining KDE with parametric modeling offers a robust framework for
quantifying the evolving radio LF of SFGs, paving the way for future work with
next-generation surveys like the SKA.

</details>


### [58] [QUEST (Quasar Unsupervised Encoder and Synthesis Tool): A machine learning framework to generate quasar spectra](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.23206)
*F. Guarneri,J. T. Schindler,R. A. Meyer,D. Yang,J. F. Hennawi,L. Lucie-Smith,S. E. I. Bosman,F. B. Davies*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于变分自编码器的模型QUEST，用于生成高红移（z > 7.0）类星体的光谱，并可生成合成测光数据和填补缺失光谱，具有良好的物理一致性和重建能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高红移类星体是研究黑洞增长与演化的重要探针，但识别困难；现有机器学习方法依赖高质量训练集，因此需要能生成逼真且多样化的类星体光谱的模型。

Method: 基于SDSS DR16Q目录，预处理并筛选出干净的类星体光谱样本，使用变分自编码器（VAE）构建QUEST模型，训练后分析其潜在空间特性，并构建生成测光和光谱重建的完整流程。

Result: 模型能准确重建输入光谱的中位数和方差，潜在空间与连续谱、光度、黑洞质量、红移、谱斜率及发射线性质相关；生成的测光数据与真实数据高度一致，黑洞质量估计准确，且能有效插值吸收线系统。

Conclusion: QUEST无需人为调参即可复现训练集中全部光谱多样性，在光谱生成、测光模拟和光谱补全方面表现优异，为高红移类星体搜寻提供了强大的数据增强工具。

Abstract: Quasars at the redshift frontier (z > 7.0) are fundamental probes of black
hole (BH) growth and evolution but notoriously difficult to identify. At these
redshifts, machine learning-based selection methods have proven to be
efficient, but require appropriate training sets to express their full
potential. Here, we present QUEST, a Variational Auto-Encoder capable of
generating realistic quasar spectra that can be post-processed for generating
synthetic photometry and for spectral imputation. We start from the SDSS DR16Q
catalogue, pre-process the spectra, and vet the sample to obtain a clean data
set. After training the model, we investigate the properties of its latent
space to understand whether it has learnt relevant physics. We provide a
pipeline to generate photometry from the sampled spectra, compare it with
actual quasar photometry, and showcase the capabilities of the model in
reconstructing and extending quasar spectra. The trained network faithfully
reproduces the input spectrum, both in terms of sample median and variance. By
examining the latent space, we find correlations with continuum and bolometric
luminosity, BH mass, redshift, continuum slope, and emission line properties.
When used to generate photometry, we find results in excellent agreement with
the control sample. The model provides satisfactory results in reconstructing
emission lines: estimates of the BH mass from the reconstructed spectra are in
good agreement with those from the original spectra. Furthermore, when spectra
with broad absorption line features are reconstructed, the model successfully
interpolates over the absorption systems. Compared with previous work, we find
excellent agreement between the spectra sampled from our model and the output
of their results. However, QUEST does not require any ad-hoc tuning, and is
capable of reproducing the full variety of spectra available in the training
set.

</details>

Abstract: Intermediate-mass black holes (IMBHs; $M_{BH} \approx 10^{3-5} M_\odot$) play

These mock HARMONI datacubes are analyzed as if they were real observations,
employing JAM within a Bayesian framework to infer IMBH masses and their
associated uncertainties. We find that ELT/HARMONI can detect the stellar
kinematic signature of an IMBH and accurately measure its mass for $M_{BH}

### [60] [Automated Exploration of Radical-Molecule Chemistry: The Case of Oxirane + CH in the ISM](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.23242)
*Moritz Bensberg,Silvia Alessandrini,Mattia Melosso,Cristina Puzzarini,Markus Reiher*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种自动化的工作流程，用于探索环氧乙烷与甲基自由基反应的势能面，旨在全面绘制其反应网络并计算主要反应通道的速率常数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 由于星际介质中分子反应网络的复杂性，传统方法难以穷尽所有反应通道，因此需要一种高效的方法来系统地探索反应势能面。

Method: 采用自动化的反应势能面探索工作流程，结合量子化学计算和动力学模拟，分析反应路径和产物分布。

Result: 确定了60个放热的双分子产物，发现主要产物为HCO自由基和乙烯，同时可能生成少量s-反式丙烯醛和2H-氧杂环丁烯；动力学模拟表明s-反式丙烯醛比甲基乙烯酮更易形成。

Abstract: Quantum chemistry provides accurate and reliable methods to investigate
reaction pathways of reactive molecular systems relevant to the interstellar
medium. However, the exhaustive exploration of a reactive network is often a
daunting task, resulting in unexplored reactive channels that affect kinetic
outcomes and branching ratios. Here, an automated workflow for exploring
reactive potential energy surfaces (PESs) is employed for the first time to
study the oxirane (C$_2$H$_4$O) plus methylidyne ($^.$CH) reaction. The
ultimate goal is to comprehensively map its PES and, subsequently, derive rate
constants for the most important reaction channels. In addition to its
astrochemical relevance, this reaction has been considered because it is a
challenging test case, its network being very extended, with 60 exothermic
bimolecular products lying below the reactant's energy. Kinetic simulations
indicate that the main product of the reaction is the HCO radical plus ethene
(C$_2$H$_4$), while formation of s-trans-propenal (acrolein) and 2H-oxene is
also possible, but to a lesser extent. Based on the present study and other
references in the literature, we suggest that the slightly higher relative
abundance of s-trans-propenal compared to methyl ketene in the interstellar
medium is a gas-phase kinetic effect, s-trans-propenal being a more easily
accessible product on the C$_3$H$_5$O$^.$ PES.

### [61] [The Velocity Map Asymmetry of Ionized Gas in MaNGA II. Correlation between Velocity Map Morphology, Star Formation, and Metallicity in Regular Disk Galaxies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.22983)
*Shuai Feng,Shiyin Shen,Yanmei Chen,Y. Sophia Dai,Jun Yin,Wenyuan Cui,Mengting Ju,Linlin Li*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 通过SDSS-IV MaNGA的积分场光谱数据，研究528个低倾角盘状星系的速度图形态、恒星形成率和气体金属丰度之间的关联，发现高速度图不对称性与偏离恒星形成主序和质量-金属丰度关系相关，表明外部贫金属气体吸积是主导机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究星系内部气体运动学如何影响其恒星形成和化学演化，特别是速度图形态与星系物理性质之间的关联。

Method: 利用MaNGA积分场光谱数据，采用谐波展开量化速度图形态，并使用全局运动学不对称性和一阶项比值作为诊断工具。

Result: 高运动学不对称性星系更易偏离恒星形成主序和质量-金属丰度关系；一阶项比值仅在低质量星系中与金属丰度相关；低于质量-金属丰度关系的星系通常具有更高的HI气体比例。

Conclusion: 外部贫金属气体吸积是导致速度图不对称性增加、金属丰度降低和恒星形成增强的主要机制，反馈外流、棒和旋臂驱动的内流及并合可能起次要作用。

Abstract: The morphology of ionized gas velocity maps provides a direct probe of the
internal gas kinematics of galaxies. Using integral field spectroscopy from
SDSS-IV MaNGA, we analyze a sample of 528 low-inclination, regular disk
galaxies to investigate the correlations between velocity map morphology, star
formation rate, and gas-phase metallicity. We quantify velocity map morphology
using harmonic expansion and adopt two complementary diagnostics: the global
kinematic asymmetry, which traces non-axisymmetric perturbations, and the
first-order term ratio, which captures axisymmetric radial motions. We find
that galaxies with higher kinematic asymmetry are more likely to deviate from
the scaling relations, typically lying either above or below the star formation
main sequence and systematically below the mass-metallicity relation. In
contrast, the first-order term ratio shows only a correlation with gas-phase
metallicity in the low-mass range and no significant dependence on star
formation rate. Moreover, galaxies below the mass-metallicity relation
generally exhibit higher HI gas fractions. These results suggest that external
gas accretion is the primary driver of the observed phenomena: inflowing
metal-poor gas increases velocity map asymmetry in disk galaxies, dilutes the
metallicity, and triggers enhanced star formation. Feedback-driven outflows,
bar- and spiral-driven inflows, and galaxy mergers may also contribute, but
likely play a secondary role.

### [62] [Spatially Resolved, Multiphase Mass Outflows of the Seyfert 1 Galaxy NGC 3227](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.23000)
*Julia Falcone,D. Michael Crenshaw,Mitchell Revalski,Travis C. Fischer,Beena Meena,Maura Kathleen Shea,Jacob Tutterow,Zo Chapman,Kesha Patel*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本研究通过多相气体外流的质量流失率分析，揭示了NGC 3227星系中心超大质量黑洞周围气体清除的时空特征，并首次计算了冷分子气体储层的空间分辨排空时间尺度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解活动星系核（AGN）外流如何影响宿主星系的气体含量及其对AGN duty cycle的潜在调控作用。

Method: 结合哈勃太空望远镜和地面望远镜的长缝光谱、[O III]成像、近红外H2发射及ALMA的CO(2-1)数据，利用Cloudy光致电离模型和发射线诊断方法，测量电离气体和分子气体的空间分辨质量外流率。

Result: 发现电离气体峰值外流率为19.9±9.2 M⊙/yr（距离SMBH 47 pc），热分子氢外流率≤9×10⁻⁴ M⊙/yr（36 pc），冷分子气体外流率≤23.1 M⊙/yr（57 pc）；冷分子气体排空时间尺度为10⁶.⁰–10⁷.⁶年，影响范围达~400 pc。

Conclusion: 多相AGN外流能有效清除NGC 3227中心数百秒差距内的气体，其时间尺度可能决定AGN的活跃周期（10⁵–10⁸年）。

Abstract: We present spatially resolved mass outflow rates of the ionized and molecular
gas in the narrow line region of the Seyfert 1 galaxy NGC 3227. Using long-slit
spectroscopy and [O III] imaging from from Hubble Space Telescope's Space
Telescope Imaging Spectrograph and Apache Point Observatory's Kitt Peak Ohio
State Multi-Object Spectrograph, in conjunction with Cloudy photoionization
models and emission line diagnostics, we find a peak ionized mass outflow rate
of $\dot M_{\text{ion}} =$ $19.9\pm9.2$ M$_\odot$ yr$^{-1}$ at a distance of
$47\pm6$ pc from the supermassive black hole (SMBH). Using archival data from
the Gemini-North Near-infrared Field Spectrograph measuring H$_2$
$\lambda2.1218$ $\mu$m emission, we find a maximum peak warm molecular outflow
rate of $\dot M_{\mathrm{H_2}} \le 9 \times 10^{-4}$ M$_\odot$ yr$^{-1}$ at a
distance of $36\pm6$ pc from the SMBH. Using archival data from the Atacama
Large Millimeter/submillimeter Array measuring CO(2-1) emission, we find a
maximum peak cold molecular gas mass outflow rate of $\dot M_{\mathrm{CO}} \le$
$23.1$ M$_\odot$ year$^{-1}$ at a distance of $57\pm6$ pc from the SMBH. For
the first time, we calculate spatially resolved gas evacuation timescales for
the cold molecular gas reservoirs ostensibly sourcing the outflows, and find
that evacuating gas to $\sim$400 pc from the SMBH occurs on timescales of
$10^{6.0} - 10^{7.6}$ years. These results indicate that the multi-phase AGN
outflows are effective in clearing the inner few hundred parsecs of NGC 3227's
gas content on timescales that may set the AGN duty cycle of $10^5 - 10^8$
years.

### [63] [Using Type-II Cepheids as Extragalactic Standard Candles: Distances to M31](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.23220)
*V. D. Pipwala,H. N. Lala,B. Lemasle,E. K. Grebel,G. Bono,G. Fiorentino*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本研究验证了II型造父变星（T2Cs）作为测量河外距离新工具的可行性，使用M31为基准星系，并采用贝叶斯稳健回归模型建立新的周光和周色关系，结果与现有方法高度一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索II型造父变星是否可作为校准河外距离尺度的新工具，特别是在缺乏年轻恒星种群的星系中补充现有标准烛光的不足。

Method: 利用LMC中的约100颗T2Cs、1000颗基模和750颗一阶振荡经典造父变星，采用贝叶斯稳健回归拟合周期-光度和周期-韦森关系，并结合巴塔恰里亚距离分类法去除M31样本中的污染源。

Result: 测得M31的距离为：使用经典造父变星为24.487±0.001（统计）±0.052（系统）mag，使用T2Cs为24.409±0.025±0.156 mag，两者均与文献值高度一致，相对精度优于98%。

Conclusion: II型造父变星可作为精确测定河外距离的有效工具，适用于JWST、LSST和ELT等下一代望远镜观测，尤其适合探测缺乏年轻星族且超出RR Lyrae探测范围的星系。

Abstract: Several standard candles have been tested and used to measure accurate
extragalactic distances over the past decades. There have been discussions
regarding the possibility of using Type-II Cepheids (T2Cs) as an alternative
tool, but rarely was this ever implemented. The aim of this project is to
assert the use of T2Cs as a new avenue for calibrating the extragalactic
distance scale, by using M31 as a benchmark galaxy. Since Ordinary Least
Squares regression methods are not immune to outliers and offer an incomplete
treatment of the uncertainties, we favor a Bayesian robust regression model to
compute new Period--Luminosity (PL) and Period--Wesenheit (PW) relations
calibrated using $\sim$100 T2Cs, $\sim$1000 fundamental-mode and $\sim$750
first-overtone classical Cepheids (CCs) in the LMC. Using these relations, we
employ a classification routine based on Bhattacharyya distances to filter out
any contaminants from the M31 sample. We validate our method by verifying that
we retrieve an accurate distance for the LMC. We find a distance to M31 of
$24.487\pm0.001$ (statistical) $\pm0.052$ (systematic) mag using CCs and of
$24.409\pm0.025$ (statistical) $\pm0.156$ (systematic) mag using T2Cs. Both
values are in excellent agreement with literature values derived from
meta-analyses, from Hubble Space Telescope (HST) observations of CCs, from the
Tip of the Red Giant Branch method, and from HST observations of RR Lyrae. In
almost all cases, we reach a relative accuracy better than 98\%, although the
archival ground-based data we use cannot compare with HST photometry. We
demonstrate that T2Cs can also be used as accurate tracers for determining
extragalactic distances, thereby making them excellent candidates for JWST,

### [67] [The Cosmic Baryon Cycle in IllustrisTNG: flows of mass, energy, and metals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.23343)
*Yossi Oren,Viraj Pandya,Rachel S. Somerville,Shy Genel,Osase Omoruyi,Amiel Sternberg*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文通过IllustrisTNG100模拟分析了星系中星际介质（ISM）和周星系介质（CGM）的质量、能量和金属的流入与流出，揭示了不同质量与红移下主导反馈机制及其对星系生长与熄火的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解星系演化过程中质量、能量和金属循环的物理机制，特别是恒星反馈和活动星系核（AGN）反馈在不同尺度和时期的作用。

Method: 利用IllustrisTNG100模拟，在晕 virial 半径（晕尺度）和ISM-CGM交界面附近（ISM尺度）的壳层中，计算超新星和AGN“动能”与“热能”模式的累积能量输入，分析流入与流出情况。

Result: 发现z≳2时，晕尺度和ISM尺度均存在净流入；后期由于大质量晕中动能AGN反馈启动，流入与流出趋于平衡，导致星系增长减缓和熄火。仅受超新星反馈主导的晕在晕尺度上缺乏预防性反馈证据，且显示快速气体再循环。风质量负载随晕质量和红移增加而减小，能量负载则几乎不变。

Conclusion: AGN反馈，尤其是动能模式，是调控星系生长和熄火的关键机制；研究结果可为半解析模型和经验模型提供指导，并深化对IllustrisTNG模拟中星系演化调控机制的理解。

Abstract: We measure and analyze the inflows and outflows of mass, energy, and metals
through the interstellar medium (ISM) and circumgalactic medium (CGM) of
galaxies in the IllustrisTNG100 simulations. We identify the dominant feedback
mechanism in bins of halo virial mass and redshift by computing the integrated
energy input from SNe and the ``kinetic'' and ``thermal'' mode of AGN feedback.
We measure all quantities in a shell at the virial radius (``halo scale'') and
one chosen to be approximately at the interface of the CGM and the interstellar
medium (ISM; ``ISM scale''). We find that galaxies have strong net positive
inflows on halo scales, and weaker but still net positive inflows on ISM
scales, at $z\gtrsim 2$. At later times, partially due to the onset of kinetic
AGN feedback in massive halos, inflows and outflows nearly balance one another,
leading to the familiar effects of the slow-down of galaxy growth and the onset
of quenching. Halos dominated by SN feedback show only weak evidence of
preventative feedback on halo scales, and we see excess ISM scale accretion
indicative of rapid gas recycling. Wind mass loadings decrease with increasing
halo mass, and with increasing redshift, while energy loadings are nearly
independent of both mass and redshift. The detailed catalogs of these mass,
metal, and energy inflow and outflow rates on galaxy and halo scales can be
used to guide empirical and semi-analytic models, and provide deeper insight
into how galaxy growth and quenching is regulated in the IllustrisTNG
simulations.

### [68] [The MiMO Catalog: Physical Parameters and Stellar Mass Functions of 1,232 Open Clusters from Gaia DR3](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.23374)
*Lu Li,Zhengyi Shao,Zhaozhou Li,Xiaoting Fu*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 提出了一种新的贝叶斯框架MiMO，利用Gaia DR3数据构建了包含1,232个星团的均匀星表，提供了精确的年龄、金属丰度、距离、消光和质量函数斜率等参数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统方法需要严格的成员星预筛选，容易遗漏成员星，影响参数估计的精度和完整性。因此需要一种能直接处理场星污染的新方法。

Method: 采用名为MiMO的新型贝叶斯框架，在颜色-星等图中对星团建模，将场星污染作为模型的一部分显式处理，无需预先筛选成员星。

Result: 得到了1,232个星团的精确参数（年龄、金属丰度、距离、消光、质量函数斜率），并提供了完整的似然链和每颗恒星的光度成员概率；识别出163个高质量的'MF Prime'子样本。

Conclusion: MiMO方法提高了星团参数估计的完整性和鲁棒性，发布的均匀星表和开源工具为星团研究提供了重要资源。

Abstract: We present a homogeneous catalog of 1,232 open clusters with precisely
determined ages, metallicities, distances, extinctions, and stellar mass
function (MF) slopes, derived from Gaia DR3 data. The parameters are inferred
using the Mixture Model for Open clusters (MiMO), a novel Bayesian framework
for modeling clusters in the color-magnitude diagram. By explicitly accounting
for field-star contamination as a model component, MiMO removes the
conventional need for stringent membership preselection, allowing for a more
complete inclusion of member stars and thereby enhancing both precision and
robustness. Our results broadly agree with existing catalogs but offer improved
precision. For each cluster, we provide the best-fit age, metallicity,
distance, extinction, and MF slope, along with their full likelihood chains and
photometric membership probabilities for individual stars. We further identify
an ``MF Prime'' subsample of 163 clusters with high-quality data, for which the
MF estimates are considered most reliable. The catalog and an open-source
implementation of MiMO are made publicly available to the community.

### [69] [Validating Open Cluster Candidates with Photometric Bayesian Evidence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.23375)
*Lu Li,Zhaozhou Li,Zhengyi Shao*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 提出基于贝叶斯框架的混合模型（MiMO）方法，利用贝叶斯因子（BF > 100）有效区分真实星团与场星涨落，实现对银河系开放星团候选体的稳健验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Gaia任务识别出的大量开放星团候选体包含显著的场星污染，传统方法难以可靠验证，需一种定量且鲁棒的统计方法来区分真实星团与假阳性。

Method: 基于MiMO混合模型，构建两个竞争模型的贝叶斯证据比较：含场星污染的单星族模型 vs 纯场星模型，通过计算贝叶斯因子（BF）评估星团存在的统计支持。

Result: 在已知星团和随机场测试中，BF > 100 的阈值能有效区分真实星团与偶然的场星密度起伏，显著提升验证可靠性。

Conclusion: 该方法为开放星团候选体提供了可量化、可扩展的验证工具，可用于星表精炼，并可推广至运动群、星流和矮卫星星系等其他解析恒星系统的多维验证。

Abstract: The thousands of open cluster (OC) candidates identified by the Gaia mission
are significantly contaminated by false positives from field star fluctuations,
posing a major validation challenge. Based on the Mixture Model for OCs (MiMO),
we present a Bayesian framework for validating OC candidates in the
color--magnitude diagram. The method compares the Bayesian evidence of two
competing models: a single stellar population with field contamination versus a
pure field population. Their ratio, the Bayes factor (BF), quantifies the
statistical support for cluster existence. Tests on confirmed clusters and
random fields show that a threshold of BF > 100 effectively distinguishes
genuine clusters from chance field overdensities. This approach provides a
robust, quantitative tool for OC validation and catalog refinement. The
framework is extendable to multi-dimensional validation incorporating
kinematics and is broadly applicable to other resolved stellar systems,
including candidate moving groups, stellar streams, and dwarf satellites.

### [70] [MIGHTEE-HI: The HI mass-stellar mass relation of massive galaxies and the HI mass function at 0.25<z<0.5](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.23406)
*Hengxing Pan,Matt J. Jarvis,Ian Heywood,Tariq Yasin,Natasha Maddox,Mario G. Santos,Maarten Baes,Anastasia A. Ponomareva,Sambatriniaina H. A. Rajohnson*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文基于MIGHTEE-HI DR1数据和恒星质量选择样本，首次利用贝叶斯堆叠技术测量了中性氢质量与恒星质量关系（M_HI-M_⋆）及其双变量分布，发现HI质量分布呈显著不对称性，并揭示了HI质量上限的存在以及高红移下最富气体星系密度可能下降的趋势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解星系中气体如何转化为恒星是星系演化研究的关键问题，而中性氢气体（HI）与恒星质量之间的关系（M_HI-M_⋆）是其中的核心环节。此前对这一关系的统计研究受限于探测灵敏度，难以准确刻画其完整分布特征，尤其是低信号区域的HI质量分布。因此，亟需更先进的统计方法和高质量观测数据来揭示该关系的真实形态及其内在分布特性。

Method: 本研究采用MIGHTEE-HI DR1的光谱数据和一个恒星质量选择的样本（0.25 < z < 0.5），利用一种强大的贝叶斯堆叠技术，测量了M_HI与M_⋆之间的关系。首次成功重建了M_⋆ > 10^9.5 M⊙星系中HI质量和恒星质量的双变量分布。同时定义并比较了⟨log₁₀(M_HI)⟩与log₁₀(⟨M_HI⟩)两个统计量，用于揭示HI质量分布的非对称性，并由此推断HI质量函数。

Result: 研究发现HI质量分布具有显著的非对称性，导致⟨log₁₀(M_HI)⟩与log₁₀(⟨M_HI⟩)之间差异可达~0.5 dex；M_HI-M_⋆关系的斜率较浅，暗示存在一个HI质量上限，超过该上限星系难以继续保留更多中性氢气体；从双变量分布推导出的HI质量函数显示，在z~0.5时，最富HI星系的共动空间密度可能已减少2-10倍。

Conclusion: 中性氢与恒星质量的关系呈现出非对称分布特征且斜率较浅，支持存在HI质量上限的物理机制；这可能意味着在z<0.5期间，大质量HI星系的数量显著减少，反映了星系气体吸积或保留能力随宇宙时间演化的趋势。

Abstract: The relationship between the already formed stellar mass in a galaxy and the
gas reservoir of neutral atomic hydrogen, is a key element in our understanding
of how gas is turned into stars in galaxy haloes. In this paper, we measure the
$M_{\rm HI}-M_{\star}$ relation based on a stellar-mass selected sample at
$0.25 < z < 0.5$ and the MIGHTEE-HI DR1 spectral data. Using a powerful
Bayesian stacking technique, for the first time we are also able to measure the
underlying bivariate distribution of HI mass and stellar mass of galaxies with
$M_\star > 10^{9.5}$ M$_{\odot}$, finding that an asymmetric underlying HI
distribution is strongly preferred by our complete samples. We define the
concepts of the average of the logarithmic HI mass, $\langle\log_{10}(M_{\rm
HI})\rangle$, and the logarithmic average of the HI mass, $\log_{10}(\langle
M_{\rm HI}\rangle)$, and find that the difference between
$\langle\log_{10}(M_{\rm HI})\rangle$ and $\log_{10}(\langle M_{\rm
HI}\rangle)$ can be as large as $\sim$0.5 dex for the preferred asymmetric HI
distribution. We observe shallow slopes in the underlying $M_{\rm
HI}-M_{\star}$ scaling relations, suggesting the presence of an upper HI mass
limit beyond which a galaxy can no longer retain further HI gas. From our
bivariate distribution we also infer the HI mass function at this redshift and
find tentative evidence for a decrease of 2-10 times in the co-moving space
density of the most HI massive galaxies up to $z\sim 0.5$.

### [71] [A targeted radio survey of infrared-selected bow shock candidates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.23470)
*M. Moutzouri,J. Mackey,N. Castro,Y. Gong,P. Jiménez-Hernández,J. A. Toalá,C. Burger-Scheidlin,M. Rugel,C. Carrasco-González,R. Brose,K. M. Menten*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 该研究利用VLA和Effelsberg射电望远镜对红外星表中的大质量恒星弓形激波候选体进行了射电巡测，结合Gaia DR3数据重新计算了驱动恒星的空间运动，在24个目标中明确探测到6个（含2个已知）并可能探测到5个，发现多数源呈非热辐射特征但统计误差较大，所有Effelsberg观测均显示为热辐射，并给出了激波层电子密度的上限及Zeta Oph弓形激波的射电辐射上限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 弓形激波主要通过红外辐射探测，而随着高灵敏度、大视场干涉仪的发展，射电探测逐渐增多。射电波段可同时探测热和非热辐射，有助于约束相对论性电子群体，因此开展多波段研究以增进对弓形激波性质的理解。

Method: 基于红外星表中的候选体，使用VLA（4-12 GHz）和Effelsberg望远镜（4-8 GHz）进行射电巡测；利用Gaia DR3重新计算驱动恒星相对于周围恒星群体的空间运动；通过射电发射图和谱指数测量分析弓形激波的射电辐射特性，并与多波段数据对比。

Result: 在24个VLA观测目标中，6个被明确探测到（包括2个先前报道的），5个可能探测到；部分目标也在Effelsberg观测中被探测到；VLA谱指数图显示大多数源为非热辐射，但统计不确定性较大，所有Effelsberg观测结果均指示为热辐射；假设为热辐射，得到了激波层内电子密度的上限；对Zeta Oph弓形激波的射电辐射给出了与MHD模拟预测相当的上限值。

Conclusion: 本次巡测显著增加了目前已知的射电辐射弓形激波数量（此前约10例），证明深度定向射电巡测能有效探测红外选证的弓形激波；建议对这些目标在更低和更高频率进行后续观测，以确认是否存在类似BD+43、BD+60和LS2355那样的非热辐射源。

Abstract: Bow shocks around massive stars have primarily been detected in IR emission,
but radio detections are becoming more frequent with the commissioning of
sensitive and large field-of-view interferometers. Radio data probes both
thermal and non-thermal emission, thereby constraining the relativistic
electron population. We undertook a radio survey for bow shocks based on IR
catalogues of candidates, using the VLA and the 100-m Effelsberg Telescope,
aiming for new detections and to better characterise the multi-wavelength
emission. We used Gaia DR3 to re-calculate spatial motion of the driving stars
with respect to the surrounding stellar population. We studied the radio
emission from bow shocks using emission maps and spectral-index measurements,
and compared our results with data from catalogues and multi-wavelength
emission. Of the 24 targets observed with the VLA in the 4-12 GHz band, six
were clearly detected (including two previously reported) and 5 possibly
detected. A subset of these were also observed and detected with Effelsberg at
4-8 GHz. The VLA-derived spectral index maps indicate non-thermal emission for
most sources, but the statistical uncertainties are large for most sources and
all Effelsberg observations indicate thermal emission. Assuming thermal
emission, we obtain upper limits on the electron density within the shocked
layer. We obtained upper limits on radio emission from the bow shock of Zeta
Oph at a similar flux level to predictions from MHD simulations. Our survey
marks a significant addition to the ca. 10 previously known radio-emitting bow
shocks in the literature, and demonstrates that deep, targeted radio surveys
can effectively detect IR-selected bow shocks. Follow-up observations of these
targets at lower and higher frequencies are encouraged to determine whether any
are non-thermal emitters like the bow shocks of BD+43, BD+60 and LS2355.
(abridged)

### [72] [Galactic bars and active galactic nucleus fuelling in the second half of cosmic history](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.23522)
*A. La Marca,M. T. Nardone,L. Wang,B. Margalef-Bentabol,S. Kruk,S. C. Trager*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本研究利用深度学习模型分析了红移至z~0.8的盘状星系中棒结构对活动星系核（AGN）的供能作用，发现棒结构显著促进了低至中等光度AGN的活动，但对高光度AGN影响甚微，暗示主并合是触发强AGN的主要机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探讨星系棒结构是否在AGN的触发和供能过程中起重要作用，特别是在不同AGN光度和相对贡献下的差异。

Method: 使用基于Galaxy Zoo志愿者分类微调的深度学习模型识别Hyper Suprime-Cam图像中的棒旋星系，并结合中红外、X射线和SED拟合三种独立方法选择AGN；通过匹配红移、恒星质量和颜色构建无棒控制样本进行对比分析。

Result: 棒旋星系中的AGN比例显著高于无棒星系，但这种效应仅存在于AGN相对贡献较低（f_AGN < 0.75）的系统中；当f_AGN > 0.75时，棒旋星系极为稀少，且AGN宿主中棒结构的比例随L_disc增加而下降。

Conclusion: 棒结构有助于低至中等光度AGN的供能，但最强的AGN主要由重大并合事件触发。

Abstract: We investigate the role of galactic bars in fuelling and triggering Active
Galactic Nucleus (AGN) in disc galaxies up to $z\sim 0.8$. We utilise a Deep
Learning model, fine-tuned on Galaxy Zoo volunteer classifications, to identify
(strongly and weakly) barred and unbarred disc galaxies in Hyper Suprime-Cam
Subaru Strategic Program $i$-band images. We select AGN using three independent
diagnostics: mid-infrared colours, X-ray detections, and spectral energy
distribution (SED) fitting. The SED analysis, performed using CIGALE,
quantifies the relative AGN contribution to the total galaxy luminosity
($f_{\rm AGN}$) and the AGN luminosity ($L_{\rm disc}$). We assess the impact
of bars by comparing AGN incidence and properties in barred galaxies against
carefully constructed redshift-, stellar mass-, and colour-matched unbarred
control samples. Our binary AGN classification experiment demonstrates that
barred disc galaxies host a statistically detectable higher fraction of AGN
compared to their unbarred counterparts, suggesting a contributing role for
bars in the global AGN budget. The contribution of bars to AGN fuelling appears
confined to systems where the AGN has a lower relative contribution to the host
galaxy's emission ($f_{\rm AGN} < 0.75$). Crucially, we find a significant
dearth of barred disc galaxies hosting AGN with $f_{\rm AGN} > 0.75$,
independent of bar strength. Consistent with this, the fraction of barred
galaxies among AGN hosts decreases with increasing $L_{\rm disc}$. Combined
with previous results, we suggest that bars contribute to fuelling the
population of low-to-moderate luminosity AGN, but major mergers are the
principal mechanism for triggering the most powerful and dominant accretion
events.

</details>


### [73] [Unveiling the collision between molecular outflows: observational evidence and hydrodynamic simulations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.23526)
*E. Cohen Arazi,P. F. Velázquez,M. E. Ortega,A. Rodríguez-González,E. Alquicira-Peláez,S. Paron,P. Rivera-Ortiz,A. Esquivel*

TL;DR: 本研究通过重新分析EGO G338.92+0.55区域的分子外流观测数据，并结合三维流体动力学模拟，提出并验证了两个外流碰撞导致该区域复杂形态和运动学特征的假设。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 利用CO发射线的矩图（0、1、2阶）进行观测数据分析，并开展三维流体动力学模拟以研究双喷流碰撞的可能性，生成合成CO图像与观测结果对比。

Result: 观测和模拟结果均显示EGO G338区域的形态和运动学特征很可能是由两个分子外流碰撞所致，合成图像与实际观测具有良好的一致性。

Conclusion: EGO G338区域的外流结构源于两个分子外流之间的碰撞，支持了外流相互作用在塑造复杂天体物理喷流结构中的重要作用。

Abstract: We present an unexplored scenario for interpreting the outflows in the EGO
G338.92+0.55 (b) region (hereafter, EGO G338). Within this framework, we
investigate the hypothesis that the interaction between two outflows is
responsible for the observed morphology and kinematics of this astrophysical
object. To explore this possibility, we reanalyse the region using
observational molecular line data. We base our analysis on maps of moments 0,
1, and 2 of the CO emission associated with the molecular outflows.
Additionally, we conduct three-dimensional hydrodynamic simulations to examine
the presence or absence of a collision between two jets. From our numerical
results, we produce synthetic CO images to facilitate a direct comparison with
observations. The findings of this study provide compelling evidence that the
observed morphology and kinematics in the EGO G338 region are the result of a
likely collision between two molecular outflows.

### [74] [The MandelZoom project II: the impact of stellar feedback on black hole accretion through an $α$-disc in dwarf galaxies with a resolved interstellar medium](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.23548)
*Eun-jin Shin,Matthew C. Smith,Debora Sijacki,Martin A. Bourne,Sophie Koudmani*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 该研究通过高分辨率模拟探讨了不同恒星反馈机制如何调控矮星系中等质量黑洞（IMBH）的成长，发现辐射反馈促进CND形成并供能IMBH，而超新星反馈抑制CND质量和吸积率，两者结合时CND间歇性存在但仍支持显著IMBH增长。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解不同恒星反馈过程对矮星系核星团中IMBH成长的影响，以准确建模IMBH的演化及其作为高红移超大质量黑洞前身的可能性。

Method: 采用超拉格朗日细化方案进行高分辨率模拟，解析α-吸积盘的自引力半径，并追踪从星际介质到黑洞的气体流入，自洽地生成核周盘（CND），比较无反馈、仅辐射反馈、仅超新星反馈及两者共存的情况。

Result: 无反馈时星系盘过度碎裂形成大质量CND；辐射反馈抑制碎裂但形成更高质量CND并增强IMBH吸积；仅超新星反馈强烈加热ISM，导致最低CND质量和吸积率；两者结合时CND间歇性存在（持续10–100 Myr后被摧毁再补充），IMBH仍显著增长且持续自转加快。

Conclusion: 精确建模多种恒星反馈的综合作用对理解IMBH成长至关重要；IMBH在各类模型中均显著增长，预示其可成为未来SKA、Rubin和LISA观测的目标，并可能是JWST观测到的高红移超大质量黑洞的前身。

Abstract: We present a suite of high-resolution simulations to study how different
stellar feedback channels regulate the growth of central intermediate-mass
black holes (IMBHs) in dwarf galaxies hosting nuclear star clusters (NSCs). We
employ a super-Lagrangian refinement scheme to resolve the self-gravity radius
of the $\alpha$-accretion disc ($<0.01$~pc) and follow the gas inflows from the
interstellar medium (ISM) to the black hole (BH), allowing for the
self-consistent emergence of circumnuclear discs (CNDs). In the absence of
stellar feedback, as expected, the galactic disc fragments excessively,
producing a massive CND. When radiative stellar feedback is included,
fragmentation is suppressed, with even more massive CNDs forming and feeding
the IMBH. With supernova (SN) feedback only, clustered SNe strongly heat the
ISM, yielding both the lowest CND masses and BH accretion rates. When both
radiative stellar feedback and SNe are included, the CND becomes intermittent:
it survives for $10$--$100$~Myr, and is then destroyed by feedback before being
replenished by fresh galactic inflows, while substantial BH growth still takes
place. These results highlight the critical importance of accurately modelling
the combined effects of key stellar feedback processes to understand IMBH
growth. Our simulation suite brackets the likely range of CND states, with
IMBHs exhibiting significant growth and systematic spin-up in all dwarf galaxy
models explored. These findings bode well for the detection of IMBHs with
future observational facilities such as SKA, the Rubin Observatory, and LISA,
and make them highly relevant progenitor candidates of the high-redshift
supermassive BHs observed by JWST.

</details>


### [75] [Cosmic Vine: High abundance of massive galaxies and dark matter halos in a forming cluster at z=3.44](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.23549)
*Nikolaj B. Sillassen,Shuowen Jin,Georgios E. Magdis,Francesco Valentino,Emanuele Daddi,Raphael Gobat,Malte Brinch,Kei Ito,Tao Wang,Hanwen Sun,Gabriel Brammer,Sune Toft,Thomas Greve*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 该研究利用JWST数据对红移z=3.44的Cosmic Vine星系原团进行了全面分析，确认了136个成员星系及一个前景结构Leaf，发现了11个宁静星系，形成迄今最早期的红序之一，揭示了高密度环境中大质量星系在宇宙早期已加速组装。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究宇宙早期星系团的形成过程，特别是大质量星系和宁静星系在高密度环境中的演化。

Method: 基于JWST DAWN数据，进行光谱确认、恒星质量函数（SMF）分析、颜色-星等图、相空间分析，并估算暗物质晕质量。

Result: 确认136个Cosmic Vine成员和47个Leaf星系；发现11个log(M*/Msun)=9.5-11.0的宁静星系，密度达场域的三倍；SMF呈头重现象，大质量星系更致密；核心晕质量为log(Mh/Msun)=13.2±0.3，子群为11.9–12.4；三个子群可能正落入核心。

Conclusion: Cosmic Vine展示了在宇宙年龄不足20亿年时，大质量星系已在大质量暗晕中快速聚集，表明高密度环境下星系演化显著加速。

Abstract: The Cosmic Vine is a massive protocluster at z=3.44 in the JWST CEERS field,
offering an ideal laboratory for studying the early phases of cluster
formation. Using the data from the DAWN JWST Archive, we conduct a
comprehensive study on the large-scale structure, stellar mass function (SMF),
quiescent members, and dark matter halos in the Cosmic Vine. First, we
spectroscopically confirm 136 galaxies in the Vine at z=3.44, and an additional
47 galaxies belonging to a diffuse foreground structure at z=3.34 which we dub

subgroups within the Leaf. Second, we identified 11 quiescent members with
log(M*/Msun)=9.5-11.0, the largest sample of quiescent galaxies in overdense
environments at z>3, which gives an enhanced quiescent galaxy number density
2x10^(-4)cMpc^(-3) that is three times above the field level at log(M*/Msun) >
10. Notably, these quiescent members form a tight red sequence on the
color-magnitude diagram, making it one of the earliest red sequences known to
date. Third, by constructing the SMFs for both star-forming and quiescent
members, we find that both SMFs are top-heavy, with a significantly enhanced
quiescent fraction at log(M*/Msun)>10.5 compared to field counterparts. The
stellar mass-size analysis reveals that star-forming members are more compact
at higher masses than their field counterparts. Finally, we estimate a halo
mass of log(Mh/Msun)=13.2+-0.3 for the protocluster core, and
log(Mh/Msun)=11.9-12.4 for satellite subgroups. The phase-space analysis
indicates that three subgroups are likely infalling to the core. This work
reveals a high abundance of massive galaxies and dark matter halos in a forming
cluster, demonstrating the accelerated assembly of massive galaxies in massive
halos when the Universe was less than 2 billion years old.

</details>

Method: 采用Kränkl和Manashov提出的方法，在MSbar方案中进行四圈重整化计算，并利用Banks-Zaks展开研究共形窗内的临界指数。

### [77] [Electroweak Baryogenesis with \texttt{BARYONET}: a self-contained review of the WKB approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.21915)
*Giulio Barni*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文采用半经典WKB方法，系统研究了电弱重子生成（EWBG）中的宇宙重子不对称性，并开发了开源代码BARYONET实现从CP破坏力推导到输运方程求解的完整流程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在建立一个自包含、可复现的EWBG理论框架，澄清现有计算中的约定并提升透明度和可重复性。

Method: 基于壁面移动参考系中的稳态Boltzmann方程，通过速度矩展开法推导出关于化学势和速度扰动的流体型耦合微分方程组，并结合CP破坏力与弱 sphaleron 源项进行求解。

Result: 成功实现了从基本推导到现象学应用的自动化流程，在单态扩展、双Higgs双重态模型和Higgs-φ⁶模型中提供了基准验证结果。

Conclusion: BARYONET为基于WKB的重子生成研究提供了一个公开、可靠且可扩展的计算平台，有助于推动该领域的标准化与协作发展。

Abstract: We present a comprehensive, self-contained pedagogical computation of the
baryon asymmetry of the Universe within electroweak baryogenesis (EWBG), from
the derivation of the semiclassical, CP-dependent force to the formulation and
solution of the transport equations obtained from the Boltzmann equations$-$all
implemented in the open-source code \texttt{BARYONET}. Our analysis follows the
semiclassical WKB approach, where spatially varying complex masses across
expanding bubble walls feel CP-violating forces that bias plasma transport.
Starting from the stationary Boltzmann equation in the wall frame and
projecting onto a hierarchy of velocity moments, we derive a compact,
fluid-like system of coupled differential equations for chemical potentials and
velocity perturbations. After obtaining the solutions, one can define the
left-handed baryon chemical potential, which acts as the source term for the
weak sphalerons. These processes generate the baryon asymmetry in front of the
wall, which is subsequently frozen once it passes through it.
  We validate the framework against established formalisms and provide
benchmarks in representative scenarios, including singlet extensions of the
Standard Model, two-Higgs-doublet models, and Higgs$-\phi^6$ constructions. The
resulting \texttt{BARYONET} implementation delivers an automated, reproducible
pipeline for WKB-based baryogenesis studies, connecting formal derivations with
phenomenological applications.
  In parallel, we revisit standard EWBG ingredients$-$\emph{diffusion
constants}, \emph{Yukawa/helicity-flip rates}, and \emph{strong/weak sphaleron
rates}$-$to clarify conventions, update numerical inputs, and present a
pedagogical derivation, ensuring transparent reproducibility.

</details>


### [78] [Superhorizon Isocurvature as a Window into Dark Matter Production](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.21917)
*Christopher Gerlach,Wolfram Ratzinger,Pedro Schwaller*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文系统地研究了在原初等曲率扰动存在的情况下，超视界曲率和等曲率扰动在长波极限下的演化，提出了一种基于第一性原理理解这些扰动本质的简单图像，并表明该机制可在暗物质的冻结产生和冻结-out模型中产生等曲率扰动，未来对物质和中微子等曲率的测量有望区分这两种机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 由于原初等曲率扰动（如独立的暗辐射区）的存在，超视界尺度下曲率扰动的演化变得复杂，需要一种不依赖繁琐宇宙扰动理论的简洁理解方式。

Method: 在长波极限下系统地重新审视超视界曲率和等曲率扰动的演化，从第一性原理出发构建简单的物理图像。

Result: 发现即使没有 sectors 之间的直接相互作用，暗辐射区的等曲率扰动也能在暴胀子 sector 中诱导出等曲率扰动；该机制可应用于简单的暗物质模型（如冻结-in 和冻结-out），并影响物质和中微子的等曲率。

Conclusion: 未来对物质和中微子等曲率扰动的观测可能有助于区分暗物质的不同产生机制，如冻结-in 与冻结-out 模型。

Abstract: In the presence of primordial isocurvature perturbations, for example in a
separate dark radiation sector, the superhorizon evolution of curvature
perturbations becomes nontrivial. If the dark sector is radiation-like and
constitutes a significant fraction of the energy density, its isocurvature can
imply isocurvature in the inflaton sector even without direct interactions
between the sectors. In this article, we revisit superhorizon curvature and
isocurvature evolution in the long-wavelength limit systematically, drawing a
simple picture of how to understand the nature of these fluctuations from first
principles and without brute-force cosmic perturbation theory. We show how the
described setup is able to source isocurvature in simple models of dark matter
such as freeze-in and freeze-out and demonstrate that future measurements of
matter and neutrino isocurvature can potentially discriminate between these two
mechanisms.

</details>


### [79] [Seafloor Topography Enhances KM3NeT Sensitivity to ANITA-like Events](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.21929)

Main category: hep-ph

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用简化的、模型无关的方法，参数化能够产生轨迹型和级联型信号的新物理过程，并结合KM3NeT/ARCA周围真实地形数据进行模拟；同时引入方位角信息以约束暗流假说下的参数空间。

Result: 发现Malta方向的海底山脉可使探测效率提升至约3倍；在包含方位角信息后，对扩散性暗流假说施加了更强限制；KM3NeT与ANITA-IV的观测可在该有效模型下同时解释，且与IceCube的冲突降低至2.4σ。

Conclusion: 地形效应对水下中微子望远镜的灵敏度有显著影响，应在未来探测器设计中予以充分考虑，类似山基探测器（如TAMBO）的做法；并提供了一套可推广到其他实验的数值计算工具。

Abstract: In this article, we introduce the concept of \textit{topographic enhancement}
in the context of ultra-high-energy neutrino detection by underwater neutrino
telescopes. We demonstrate that the local topography around KM3NeT/ARCA can
increase the detection efficiency in scenarios involving long-lived particles
by up to a factor of $\sim 3$ due to the presence of an underwater mountain
range in the direction of Malta. We consider a simplified model-independent
approach that parametrizes the new physics able to generate both track-like and
cascade-like signals in neutrino telescopes. When explaining the KM3-230213A
event with a diffuse dark flux hypothesis, including its azimuthal
direction--in addition to the zenith angle--provides additional constraints on
the parameter space. In this effective model, the observations by KM3NeT and
ANITA-IV can be simultaneously explained and the global tension with the lack
of a corresponding detection in IceCube is reduced to 2.4 sigma. This work
underscores the importance of incorporating topographic effects in the design
and optimization of next-generation neutrino telescopes, as is done in the
context of mountain-based detectors such as TAMBO. We present a numerical code
which can be used to easily extend this topographical analysis to other
experiments.

### [80] [Bubble wall velocity with out-of-equilibrium corrections](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.21942)
*Carlo Branchina,Angela Conaci,Stefania De Curtis,Luigi Delle Rose*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该论文研究了宇宙学一阶电弱相变中气泡壁传播的非平衡效应，发现非平衡修正显著增强了气泡壁的有效摩擦，导致更慢的壁速度和更宽的壁轮廓，从而提升电弱重子生成效率并增强未来引力波探测的可能性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解非平衡效应对电弱相变中气泡壁动力学的影响，以更准确地描述宇宙早期相变过程及其对可观测量的影响。

Method: 超越局域热平衡近似，数值求解标量场、流体力学和玻尔兹曼方程的耦合系统，采用谱方法对碰撞积分进行第一性原理处理。

Result: 在单态扩展标准模型下，非平衡效应显著增强有效摩擦，导致气泡壁速度减慢、壁轮廓变宽，并增强电弱重子生成效率。

Conclusion: 非平衡效应在电弱相变中起关键作用，显著影响气泡壁传播和相关宇宙学观测量，提升了重子不对称生成在现实参数空间中的可行性。

Abstract: We study how out-of-equilibrium effects modify the steady-state propagation
of bubble walls during a cosmological first-order electroweak phase transition.
Going beyond the local thermal equilibrium approximation, we numerically solve
the coupled system of scalar field, hydrodynamic and Boltzmann equations using
a spectral algorithm that allows a first-principle treatment of the collision
integral. This approach enables a quantitative assessment of non-equilibrium
perturbations in the plasma and their backreaction on the wall motion. Focusing
on the singlet extension of the Standard Model as a minimal benchmark scenario,
we find that out-of-equilibrium corrections substantially enhance the effective
friction on the expanding front, leading to slower wall velocities and broader
wall profiles compared to the equilibrium case. These modifications have
significant implications for cosmological observables. For instance, they
enhance the efficiency of electroweak baryogenesis, thus improving the
viability of baryon asymmetry generation within realistic parameter regions
that can also be probed by future gravitational wave interferometers.

Result: 发现若不考虑中微子波包的有限尺寸，弱相互作用在连续极限下趋于平凡；而波包尺寸对密集环境中的中微子散射具有关键影响。

  <summary>Details</summary>

density, serves as a unique laboratory for new-physics searches. Low-energy
supernovae (LESNe) provide particularly powerful probes, as their low explosion
energies place stringent limits on any additional energy deposition in the
mantle by new particles. We present refined LESN constraints on
lepton-flavor-violating (LFV) axions and axion-like particles (ALPs) with

scattering, the last of which is investigated here for the first time in the
context of LFV-ALPs. We find that muon decay dominates in the low-mass regime,

in the intermediate-mass range. To derive accurate limits, we compute both the
energy transfer from the SN core to the mantle and the energy loss due to ALP
production in the mantle, which can be substantial for both large and small
couplings -- the latter case, to our knowledge, not previously noted in the

strengthen previous SN bounds and highlight the exceptional sensitivity of

of non-perturbative Quantum Chromodynamics. We investigate the conditions for

TL;DR: 本文在有限温度QCD求和规则框架下研究了重矢量和轴矢介子（$J/\psi$、$\Upsilon$ 和 $B_c$）的热行为，利用更新的PDG-2024夸克质量、现代格点QCD输入的胶子凝聚态以及温度依赖的连续谱阈值，计算了其质量和衰变常数随温度的演化。结果与实验和LHCb数据吻合良好，并揭示了近临界温度下的抑制层次结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解重夸克偶素在有限温度下的性质对于探知QCD相变及强相互作用介质中的束缚态行为至关重要。现有理论在结合最新实验数据和格点QCD信息方面仍有改进空间，因此需要更精确的有限温度QCD求和规则分析。

Method: 采用有限温度QCD求和规则方法，结合更新的PDG-2024夸克质量、格点QCD支持的胶子凝聚态以及由真空稳定性约束的温度依赖连续谱阈值，计算了$J/\psi$、$\Upsilon$和$B_c$介子的质量$m(T)$和衰变常数$f(T)$在$T/T_c \lesssim 0.9$范围内的演化。

Result: 零温极限下计算结果与实验及LHCb测量值偏差在1%以内；临近临界温度时，介子的相对抑制呈现$\Upsilon < J/\psi < B_c$的层次结构，与结合能和格点谱趋势一致；预测的$B_c$系统$1P$--$1S$分裂为0.477 GeV，与LHCb观测相符。

Conclusion: 该工作提供了重介子在有限温度下的一致理论基线，揭示了抑制行为的物理机制，为未来包含辐射修正、高维算符和宽度效应的扩展研究奠定了基础。

Abstract: We analyze the thermal behavior of heavy vector and axial-vector mesons
($J/\psi$, $\Upsilon$, and $B_c$) within the finite-temperature QCD sum-rule
framework. Using updated PDG-2024 quark masses, modern lattice-informed gluon
condensates, and a temperature-dependent continuum threshold constrained by
vacuum stability, we compute the evolution of the masses $m(T)$ and decay
constants $f(T)$ up to $T/T_c \lesssim 0.9$. The extracted zero-temperature
limits reproduce experimental and LHCb values within 1\%. Near the critical
temperature, the relative suppression follows a clear hierarchy $\Upsilon <
J/\psi < B_c$, consistent with their binding energies and lattice spectral
trends. The predicted $1P$--$1S$ splitting for the $B_c$ system,
$0.477~\mathrm{GeV}$, matches the LHCb observation of orbitally excited
$B_c^{+}$ states. The results provide a coherent finite-temperature baseline
for future extensions including radiative, higher-dimensional, and width
effects.

Abstract: The strong CP problem remains one of the most important unresolved issues in

the problem by assuming that CP is an exact symmetry of the Lagrangian but

observed Cabibbo-Kobayashi-Maskawa (CKM) phase without reintroducing a nonzero

construct a model in which CP is spontaneously broken at an intermediate scale
along pseudo-flat directions, stabilized by soft SUSY breaking and
non-perturbative effects of a gauge theory. The latter setup predicts light
scalars in the SCPV sector whose masses are determined by the SUSY breaking
scale.

future colliders such as the FCC-ee and CEPC. The SM predicts a one-loop

results yield upper limits on the anomalous couplings, from which we infer
branching ratios for $Z \to \nu\bar{\nu}\gamma$ on the order of $10^{-9}$. This
represents a significant improvement of several orders of magnitude over the
LEP sensitivity. Consequently, this study demonstrates the unique potential of
the Tera-Z runs not only to test the SM loop-level predictions with
unprecedented precision but also to tightly constrain or reveal new anomalous

TL;DR: 本文研究了在反中微子-质子反应中产生超子、粲重子及潜在的强子分子态的过程，利用有效拉格朗日量、手征微扰理论和强子分子模型进行了理论计算。结果表明，未来的中微子设施可作为探索奇异和粲夸克领域中强相互作用动力学及 exotic 重子态的补充平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索在干净末态的反中微子-质子反应中产生奇异和粲重子以及可能的强子分子态，以提供对强相互作用在奇异和粲夸克领域中的理解。

Method: 采用有效拉格朗日方法、手征微扰理论和强子分子模型，对多个相关通道进行理论计算，包括可能导致强子分子态(\bar{D}N)形成的通道。

Result: 理论计算结果显示，在\bar{\nu}_\mu p反应中可观测到超子、粲重子及(\bar{D}N)类强子分子候选态的产生，某些通道具有可观的截面。

Conclusion: 未来中微子实验设施有望成为研究 exotic 重子态和强相互作用动力学的重要且互补的平台，尤其适用于奇异和粲夸克相关的非微扰QCD研究。

Abstract: We investigate the production of hyperons, charmed baryons, and potential
hadronic molecular states in neutrino-proton ($\bar{\nu}_\mu p$) reaction, a
process characterized by a particularly clean final state. Employing effective
Lagrangians, chiral perturbation theory, and a hadronic molecular model, we
perform theoretical calculations for several relevant channels, including those
leading to the formation of the hadronic molecular candidate $(\bar{D}N)$. Our
results indicate that future neutrino facilities could serve as a complementary
platform for exploring exotic baryonic states and provide valuable insights
into the dynamics of strong interactions in the strange and charm sectors.

### [102] [Investigation of Resonances in the $Σ({1/2}^{-})$ System Based on the Chiral Quark Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.23378)
*Yu Yao,Xuejie Liu,Xiaoyun Chen,Yuheng Wu,Jialun Ping,Yue Tan,Qi Huang*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本研究在手征夸克模型框架下，采用高斯展开方法研究Σ(1/2⁻)系统的三夸克和五夸克态共振结构，发现两个能量约为1.8 GeV的三夸克态可对应实验观测的Σ(1750)和Σ(1900)，五夸克组态中存在Σπ、N̄K和N̄K*等稳定共振态，支持Σ(1/2⁻)系统具有双极结构，主要由Σπ和N̄K构成，主衰变道为Λπ，而N̄K*需与三夸克成分混合才能更好解释实验数据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究Σ(1/2⁻)共振态的内部结构，特别是是否存在多夸克组态及双极结构，以理解其与实验观测态如Σ(1750)和Σ(1900)的关系。

Method: 在手征夸克模型中使用高斯展开方法构建多夸克态轨道波函数，并通过两组参数拟合减少模型依赖性，结合复伸缩方法进行耦合道计算。

Result: 三夸克计算中得到两个Σ(1/2⁻)态（~1.8 GeV），对应Σ(1750)和Σ(1900)；五夸克组态中发现稳定的Σπ、N̄K和N̄K*共振态，其中Σπ和N̄K形成双极结构，主衰变为Λπ；N̄K*态宽度与实验不符，需混合三夸克成分。

Conclusion: Σ(1/2⁻)系统存在双极结构，主要由Σπ和N̄K主导，支持类似于Λ(1380)-Λ(1405)的分子态图像；Σ(1750)和Σ(1900)可能包含显著的五夸克成分，N̄K*态需与三夸克态混合才能解释实验结果。

Abstract: In this work, we investigate the resonance structures in the $\Sigma(1/2^-)$
system from both three-quark and five-quark perspectives within the framework
of the chiral quark model. An accurate few-body computational approach, the
Gaussian Expansion Method, is employed to construct the orbital wave functions
of multiquark states. To reduce the model dependence on parameters, we fit two
sets of parameters to check the stability of the results. The calculations show
that our results remain stable despite changes in the parameters. In the
three-quark calculations, two $\Sigma(1/2^-)$ states are obtained with energies
around 1.8~GeV, which are good candidates for the experimentally observed
$\Sigma(1750)$ and $\Sigma(1900)$. In the five-quark configuration, several
stable resonance states are identified, including $\Sigma \pi$, $N \bar{K}$,
and $N \bar{K}^{*}$. These resonance states survive the channel-coupling
calculations under the complex-scaling framework and manifest as stable
structures. Our results support the existence of a two-pole structure for the
$\Sigma(1/2^-)$ system, predominantly composed of $\Sigma \pi$ and $N \bar{K}$
configurations, analogous to the well-known $\Lambda(1380)$-$\Lambda(1405)$
($\Sigma \pi$-$N \bar{K}$) system. On the other hand, although the energy of
the $N \bar{K}^{*}$ configuration is close to that of $\Sigma(1750)$ and
$\Sigma(1900)$, the obtained width is not consistent with the experimental
values. This suggests that the $N \bar{K}^{*}$ state needs to mix with
three-quark components to better explain the experimental $\Sigma(1750)$ and
$\Sigma(1900)$ states. According to our decay width calculations, the predicted
two resonance states are primarily composed of $\Sigma \pi$ and $N \bar{K}$,
with their main decay channel being $\Lambda \pi$.

</details>

Result: 模型中自旋无关的暗物质-核子散射振幅被动量转移抑制，符合pNG暗物质特征；在特定参数区域可同时满足热产生机制和当前观测丰度，并避开直接探测实验的严格限制。

Conclusion: 该六维U(1)$_\chi$磁化紧致化模型提供了一种自然的pNG暗物质实现方式，兼具理论简洁性与实验兼容性。

Abstract: We study a six-dimensional U(1)$_\chi$ gauge theory compactified on a

without introducing an additional scalar field. We show that the leading
spin-independent DM-nucleus amplitude is suppressed by momentum transfer in our

be considered in this endeavour. A commensurate effort from the theory
community will be needed to interpret future measurements. I present an
overview of the broad potential of the FCC-ee flavour physics program.

### [107] [Pinched geometries in $\mathbf{2}$D Lorentzian quantum Regge calculus](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.22596)
*Yoshiyasu Ito,Daisuke Kadoh,Yuki Sato*

TL;DR: 研究了在固定时空面积下具有无限时间延展的pinched几何在二维洛伦兹量子Regge演算模型中的行为，使用张量重整化群方法发现此类几何在三角形数量趋于无穷时被强烈抑制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用张量重整化群（TRG）方法，结合不同的积分测度和三角剖分方案，分析pinched几何在大量三角形极限下的行为。

Result: 结果显示pinched几何在各种测度和三角化下均被强烈抑制，表明平滑几何可能浮现，并显示出在无穷三角形极限下的某种普适性。

Conclusion: pinched几何在所研究的量子Regge演算模型中不占主导地位，支持平滑时空结构的出现和模型的普适性。

Abstract: We investigate pinched geometries in a two-dimensional Lorentzian model of

method. A pinched geometry refers to a configuration with an infinitely long
temporal extent, even when the total spacetime area is fixed. We examine
several choices of integration measures and triangulations to study whether
such geometries can dominate in the limit of infinitely many triangles. Our
results indicate that pinched geometries are strongly suppressed, and this
suppression is observed across different integral measures and triangulations.
These results suggest the possible emergence of smooth geometries as well as a
sort of universality for infinitely many triangles.

### [108] [A gauge invariant Hamiltonian evolution across the black hole horizon in asymptotically AdS spacetimes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.21920)
*Anurag Kaushal,Naveen S. Prabhakar,Spenta R. Wadia*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 研究了反德西特时空（AAdS）中黑洞背景下探测标量场的量子动力学，采用最大切片规范下的哈密顿形式，自然导出了纠缠的Hartle-Hawking态，并给出了描述算符在两个CFT乘积空间中时间演化的含时厄米哈密顿量，实现了视界穿越激发的幺正描述，同时提供了边界理论中指示视界穿越的序参量重构公式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解黑洞背景中量子场的动力学行为，尤其是在最大切片规范下如何实现视界穿越的幺正演化，并探索全息对偶中边界理论对体物理的重构能力。

Method: 在最大切片规范的虫洞坐标下求解Klein-Gordon方程，将标量场展开为归一化解的叠加，使用两个边界CFT乘积空间中的算符构造量子态与哈密顿量，并计算体Wightman两点半函数。

Result: 得到了一个良定义的含时厄米哈密顿量，其作用于HH态产生有限范数态，实现了视界穿越激发的幺正演化；提出了边界序参量的体重构公式；计算了双侧BTZ黑洞中跨内外区的两点半函数，发现其在大时间极限下趋于非零常数。

Conclusion: 在最大切片规范下，通过CFT乘积空间可实现黑洞内部量子态的幺正演化和体-边全息重构，支持了视界穿越过程的量子一致性。

Abstract: We study the quantum dynamics of a probe scalar field in the background of a
black hole in AAdS spacetime in the Hamiltonian formulation of general
relativity in the maximal slicing gauge. The black hole solution in this gauge
is expressed in terms of wormhole coordinates, a smooth coordinate system with
constant time slices that cut across the horizon, and asymptote to the Killing
time slices at the boundaries.
  The quantum scalar field is expanded in terms of normalized solutions of the
Klein-Gordon equation, that are valid at all points in spacetime. The operators
that appear in the expansion are in the product space of the CFTs on the two
spacetime boundaries, which are by definition gauge invariant under small bulk
diffeomorphisms. The entangled Hartle-Hawking (HH) state arises naturally from
this construction.
  One of our main results is a well defined formula for the time dependent
Hermitian Hamiltonian of the probe scalar in the product space of the two CFTs,
which describes the time development of operators/states along the maximal
slices. This Hamiltonian acting on the HH state creates a state of finite norm.
Consequently there is a unitary description of horizon crossing scalar field
excitations on top of the HH state. We also present a bulk reconstruction
formula that evaluates an order parameter that signals horizon crossing in the
boundary theory.
  We calculate various bulk Wightman two-point functions on the two-sided BTZ
black hole. We recover Hawking's thermodynamic results in the exterior region
when expressed in terms of BTZ coordinates that are related to the wormhole
coordinates by a singular transformation. We compute the two-point function
with one insertion in the future/past interior and the other in the exterior.
Both are related by a time reflection symmetry and asymptote to a non-zero
constant as the coordinate time between the two points becomes large.

### [109] [Constrained instantons in scalar field theories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.21922)
*Benjamin Elder,Kinga Gawrych,Arttu Rajantie*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文重新审视了Affleck于1981年提出的约束瞬子思想，并将其发展为一种完整的计算方法，用于处理不存在传统鞍点的理论中的真空衰变率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在某些量子场论中不存在局域化的鞍点（即时子），这使得传统的非微扰分析方法失效，因此需要发展新的方法来描述这些理论中的真空衰变等非微扰现象。

Method: 采用约束瞬子方法，通过引入两种不同的约束条件，数值求解场方程，并通过负模数分析识别出约束瞬子解和作用量极小值解。

Result: 发现了解的双分支结构：一个分支对应约束瞬子，另一个对应约束下的作用量极小值；并讨论了它们对真空衰变率计算的意义。

Conclusion: 约束瞬子方法为在缺乏传统鞍点的理论中计算真空衰变率提供了一个可行且系统的框架。

Abstract: Instantons, localised saddle points of the action, play an important role in
describing non-perturbative aspects of quantum field theories, for example
vacuum decay or violation of conservation laws associated with anomalous
symmetries. However, there are theories in which no saddle point exists. In
this paper, we revisit the idea of constrained instantons, proposed initially
by Affleck in 1981, and develop it into a complete method for computing the
vacuum decay rate in such cases. We apply this approach to the massive scalar
field theory with a negative quartic self-interaction using two different
constraints. We solve the field equations numerically and find a two-branch
structure, with two distinct solutions for each value of the constraint. By
counting the negative modes, we identify one branch of solutions as the
constrained instantons and the other as the minima of the action subject to the
constraint. We discuss their significance for the computation of the vacuum
decay rate.

</details>


### [110] [2+1 dimensional gravity in AAdS spacetimes with spatial wormhole slices: Reduced phase space dynamics and the BTZ black hole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.21923)
*Anurag Kaushal,Naveen S. Prabhakar,Spenta R. Wadia*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究2+1维渐近AdS时空中引力系统的哈密顿结构，解决规范不变性问题，并探讨其经典与量子动力学行为，特别是与BTZ黑洞的关系。

Method: 采用哈密顿形式求解爱因斯坦方程，固定最大切片和空间调和规范，求解约束方程并构造约化相空间；分析边界ADM哈密顿量对应的薛定谔方程及其量子化。

Result: 获得二维约化相空间；得出连续正能谱的量子态，每个能量本征值E对应一个BTZ黑洞（质量M=E/2）；经典解对应于双边BTZ黑洞经微分同胚变换后的时空。

Conclusion: 该模型成功描述了2+1维AAdS引力系统在特定规范下的完全可积结构，量子化后自然导出BTZ黑洞谱，支持全息原理下边界时间演化与体时空的对应关系。

Abstract: We solve Einstein's equations with negative cosmological constant in $2+1$
dimensions in the Hamiltonian formulation. The spacetime has the topology of
$\Sigma \times \mathbf{R}$ where $\mathbf{R}$ corresponds to the time direction
and $\Sigma$ is a cylinder $\mathbf{R} \times \mathbf{S}^1$ and the spacetime
metric satisfies asymptotically AdS (AAdS) boundary conditions.
  We address the question of gauge invariance by fixing the maximal slicing and
spatial harmonic gauge conditions and demonstrate that there are no residual
small diffeomorphisms in this gauge. We explicitly solve the Hamiltonian and
momentum constraints, and the gauge conditions to obtain a two dimensional
reduced phase space. For simplicity, and with the BTZ black hole in mind, we
restrict the solution of the momentum constraints to be independent of
$\mathbf{S}^1$.
  In AAdS spacetimes besides the standard Wheeler-deWitt equations there is a
Schroedinger equation corresponding to the boundary ADM Hamiltonian. We express
this Hamiltonian in terms of the reduced phase space variables and discuss its
classical solutions and quantization. We exhibit the wave functions and a
continuous positive energy spectrum. Each energy eigenvalue $E$ corresponds to
a BTZ black hole of mass $M=E/2$. This identification is based on the fact that
the classical solution of the reduced phase space dynamics gives rise to a
spacetime that is related to the two-sided BTZ black hole by a diffeomorphism.

</details>

*Ofer Aharony,Suman Kundu,Tal Sheaffer*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个弦理论，作为二维零耦合Yang-Mills理论（可视为BF理论）的对偶，并通过引入具有特定边界条件的弦世界面，成功计算了Wilson圈的期望值，验证了其与已知Yang-Mills结果的一致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了理解二维Yang-Mills理论在零耦合下的全息对偶，扩展此前提出的弦理论框架，以涵盖Wilson圈等非局域算符的计算。

Method: 通过在Polyakov-like推广的Hořava拓扑刚性弦理论中引入带有Dirichlet和Neumann边界条件的世界面边界，计算不同拓扑构型下的Wilson圈期望值，并在非共形规范下处理含反定向管或自交环的情况。

Result: 弦理论在包括分支点、反定向管和自交Wilson圈等多种非平凡例子中，均精确复现了已知的Yang-Mills理论结果。

Conclusion: 该弦理论是二维零耦合Yang-Mills理论的有效对偶描述，能够统一处理复杂拓扑结构和非局域可观测量。

Abstract: In earlier work we proposed a string theory dual to two dimensional
Yang-Mills theory at zero coupling (which can also be thought of as a $BF$
theory), given by a Polyakov-like generalization of Ho\v rava's topological
rigid string theory, and we showed that it correctly reproduces (in the $1/N$
expansion) several partition functions of $SU(N)$ Yang-Mills theory. In the
present paper, we generalise this to Wilson loop expectation values by adding
boundaries with one Dirichlet and one Neumann boundary condition to our string
worldsheets. We discuss in detail several examples, including examples where
the worldsheet has branch points or orientation-reversing tubes, or where the
Wilson loop has one or more self-intersections, and we show that in all of them
the string theory reproduces the known Yang-Mills expectation values. We argue
that examples with orientation-reversing tubes or self-intersecting Wilson
loops cannot be brought to the conformal gauge, so we analyse them in a
different gauge.

### [113] [Four-dimensional topological Yang-Mills-Higgs theories with BRST instability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.22323)
*Guilherme Sadovski*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了四维拓扑杨-米尔斯理论在耦合类似希格斯场后的表示形式，发现其在非平凡模空间邻域内可表现为有质量的规范场。伴随表示中存在高于树图阶的BRST不稳定性，类似于Coleman-Weinberg机制；基本表示需实化SU(N)到SO(2N)，并在树图阶即表现出更强的不稳定性。伴随情况普遍存在稳定的拓扑孤子（顶点/单极子），这些不稳定性表明局部自由度重新进入物理谱。实化基本情形可能为四维拓扑引力模型提供新框架，并为无非平凡Gribov问题的非阿贝尔规范理论中BRST对称性破缺提供了罕见实例。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索四维拓扑场论在引入Higgs-like场后的动力学行为，特别是BRST对称性是否稳定以及局部自由度是否会重现，旨在理解拓扑理论向物理理论过渡的可能性，并寻找可用于4d拓扑引力的新模型。

Method: 通过将拓扑Yang-Mills理论与Higgs-like场耦合，分析其在不同表示（伴随表示和基本表示）下的量子行为，利用BRST对称性分析和模空间结构研究不稳定性机制，并比较Coleman-Weinberg机制与观察到的现象。

Result: 发现伴随表示中存在高于树图阶的BRST不稳定性，类似Coleman-Weinberg机制；基本表示经SU(N)→SO(2N)实化后在树图阶即出现显著不稳定性；伴随表示中存在稳定的拓扑孤子；这些结果表明局部自由度被重新引入物理谱，且实化基本情形可能适用于4d拓扑引力模型。此外，提供了非阿贝尔规范理论中BRST对称性破缺但Gribov问题平凡的罕见例子。

Conclusion: 四维拓扑Yang-Mills理论在适当耦合Higgs-like场后会失去严格的拓扑性，因BRST对称性破缺而引入局部物理自由度，这既限制了其作为纯粹拓扑理论的应用，也为构建如4d拓扑引力等新物理模型提供了潜在路径。

Abstract: We show that four-dimensional topological Yang-Mills theories, when suitably
coupled to Higgs-like fields, admit representations in terms of massive gauge
fields in a non-trivial neighborhood of the minima moduli. In the adjoint
representation, BRST instability is present beyond tree-level, and closely
resembles the Coleman-Weinberg mechanism. The fundamental representation
requires realification $SU(N) \hookrightarrow SO(2N)$, but exhibits a more
pronounced instability at tree-level. Stable topological solitons
(vertices/monopoles) are generically present in the adjoint case. These
instabilities indicate the reintroduction of local degrees of freedom into the
physical spectrum of these topological field theories. In particular, the
realified fundamental case may provide a promising framework for 4d topological
gravity models. In addition, our results offer rare examples of BRST symmetry
breaking in non-Abelian gauge theories with trivial Gribov problems.

Abstract: Continuing the formulation of finite $N$ Hilbert spaces in emergent theories

reducing the construction to linear algebra. As a stringent check, of our

gauge invariant operators with no redundancies. This results in a reduction of
the Hilbert space, in particular the gauge invariant secondary invariants
realize an emergent Fock space with finite-$N$ occupation-numbers.

### [118] [Toward Krylov-based holography in double-scaled SYK](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.22658)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 利用DSSYK模型的双尺度极限，结合共形态中的期望值计算、体重构方法以及第三量化框架下的婴儿宇宙模型，分析Krylov复杂性及其高阶变体与体几何量之间的对偶关系。

Result: 发现了Krylov复杂性增长率与虫洞速度及下落粒子固有动量之间的三重对偶；高阶Krylov复杂性反映复制虫洞的连通贡献；对数形式探测复制鞍点结构；Krylov熵等于迹去婴儿宇宙后的母几何密度矩阵的冯·诺依曼熵。

Abstract: Building on the duality between Krylov complexity and geodesic length in
Jackiw-Teitelboim and sine-dilaton gravity, we develop a precise holographic
dictionary for quantities in the Krylov subspace of the double-scaled
Sachdev-Ye-Kitaev model (DSSYK). First, we demonstrate that the growth rate of
Krylov state complexity corresponds to the wormhole velocity, and show that its
expectation value in coherent states serves as a boundary diagnostic of
firewall-like structures via bulk reconstruction. We also delineate an
alternative bulk description in terms of the proper momentum of an infalling
particle at early times, establishing a threefold duality between the Krylov
complexity growth rate, wormhole velocity, and proper momentum, with clear
regimes of validity. Beyond the first moments, we argue that higher-order

wormholes, while the logarithmic variant probes the replica saddle structure.
Finally, within a third-quantized setting incorporating baby universes, we show
that the Krylov entropy equals the von Neumann entropy of the parent-geometry
density matrix obtained after tracing out baby universes, thereby quantifying
information flow into the baby universe sector. Together, these results elevate
Krylov-space observables to sharp probes of bulk dynamics and topology in
ensemble-averaged 2D gravity.

### [119] [Local gauge invariant operator on isometry breaking background](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.22879)
*Min-Seok Seo*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文探讨了在引力理论中如何通过自发破缺等距对称性来构造局域规范不变算符，利用Stückelberg机制将度规和物质涨落结合，并指出即使存在此类算符，晚期时空涨落的累积仍可能阻碍黑洞信息悖论中‘岛’区域的可靠构建。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决局域场算符与引力的微分同胚不变性之间的不兼容问题，特别是在量子力学与狭义相对论协调成功但难以推广到引力背景下的情况下。

Method: 引入自发破缺等距对称性的背景几何，通过Stückelberg机制构造局域规范不变算符，并类比引入时钟和尺子的概念；分析时间或空间等距对称性破缺下的曲率扰动。

Result: 成功构造了在等距对称性自发破缺背景下的局域规范不变算符，例如准德西特空间中的曲率扰动；发现时空点涨落在长时间内累积，可能导致永恒暴胀，并影响局部区域（如岛）上规范不变算符的可靠构造。

Conclusion: 为实现真正局域且规范不变的物理量，需强破缺背景对称性，例如在蒸发黑洞中可能需要向高维黑洞转变以抑制晚期涨落。

Abstract: Whereas local field operators play the crucial role in reconciling quantum
mechanics and special relativity, they are not trivially compatible with the
diffeomorphism invariance of gravity. In order to address this issue, we
consider the background geometry which breaks the isometry spontaneously. Then
the local gauge invariant operator can be constructed through the St\"uckelberg
mechanism, where the fluctuation of the metric in the direction of the isometry
breaking combines with that of matter whose classical solution breaks the
isometry. This is equivalent to introducing the clock and the rod to promote
the local field operators to the gauge invariant ones. A typical example is the
curvature perturbation in quasi-de Sitter space arising from the spontaneous
breaking of the timelike isometry. We also discuss the features of the local
gauge invariant operator when the spacelike isometry is spontaneously broken.
Meanwhile, even if the local gauge invariant operators exist, it does not
guarantee the reliable construction of the gauge invariant operators on the
local region like the island, which is regarded as an essential ingredient to
resolve the black hole information paradox. This is because the fluctuation of
the spacetime point is accumulated in time, which in fact also gives rise to
eternal inflation in quasi-de Sitter space. In order to suppress the
fluctuation at late time, the isometry must be strongly broken by the
background. In the case of the evaporating black hole, it may be achieved by
the transition to the higher dimensional black hole.

</details>


### [120] [A study of string theory and the AdS/CFT correspondence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.22906)
*Pedro Bairrão*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文综述了Maldacena关于AdS/CFT对应关系的原始推导及理解该理论所需的弦论主要内容，重点包括Yang-Mills理论的大N展开、玻色弦理论、D-膜性质及其相互作用，并讨论了超弦理论与超引力的联系以及AdS/CFT对偶的基本性质和全息字典概念。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 成功复现了闭开弦对偶，验证了D-膜间相互作用；展示了II型超弦低能谱与十维II型超引力的一致性；完整呈现了AdS/CFT对偶的原始推导及其全息性质。

Abstract: This dissertation consists of a comprehensive and pedagogical review of
Maldacena's original derivation of the AdS/CFT correspondence and the main
topics of string theory necessary to understand it. The large $N$ expansion of
Yang-Mills theory is presented as the main motivation for seeking a
string-theoretic language for gauge theories. The bosonic string is studied in
conformal gauge, with an emphasis on the spectrum and the low energy effective
actions for both closed and open strings. The properties of D-branes are
studied via T-duality, and closed-open string duality is checked by explicitly
computing the interaction amplitude between two D-branes. The type II
superstring theories are studied in the RNS formalism and their massless
spectrum is shown to match that of the type II ten-dimensional supergravity
theories. Supersymmetric branes are discussed, including their realization as
supergravity solitons, and the original derivation of the AdS/CFT duality is
presented. Some of the properties of the correspondence are discussed,
including the idea of the holographic dictionary.

### [121] [The anomalous spin-statistics connection arising from pseudo-Hermiticity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.22952)
*Yao Bai,Cheng-Yang Lee,Ruifeng Leng,Siyi Zhou*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出了一类自由伪厄米量子场论的新自旋统计定理，其中整数自旋粒子表现为费米统计，半整数自旋粒子表现为玻色统计，与传统情况相反。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统自旋统计定理在伪厄米量子场论中不适用，需要建立新的理论框架以解释非厄米系统中的统计行为。

Method: 通过使用伪厄米共轭而非厄米共轭来定义正则场算符，推导出自由伪厄米量子场的自旋与统计关系，并保持局域性、洛伦兹协变性和幺正演化。

Result: 发现整数自旋场呈现费米子统计，半整数自旋场呈现玻色子统计，且自由场满足基本物理原理，但相互作用可能导致幺正性破坏。

Conclusion: 该框架成功绕开了传统自旋统计定理，为非厄米量子场论提供了新的统计规律，同时提出了在相互作用理论中恢复幺正性的可能途径。

Abstract: We establish a new spin-statistics theorem for a class of free
pseudo-Hermitian quantum field theories whose particles furnish unitary
irreducible representations of the Poincar\'{e} group. In this framework, free
pseudo-Hermitian fields with integer spin exhibit fermionic statistics, whereas
those with half-integer spin exhibit bosonic statistics, opposite to the
conventional case. This reversal arises from defining canonical field operators
using pseudo-Hermitian conjugation rather than Hermitian conjugation, thereby
circumventing the conventional spin-statistics theorem. The free fields retain
locality, Lorentz covariance, and unitary evolution. However, interactions may
violate unitarity due to the intrinsically non-Hermitian nature of the full
Hamiltonian. We discuss potential resolutions to restore unitarity in
interacting theories.

</details>

*Joon-Hwi Kim*

Method: 利用ambitwistor空间作为无质量粒子的相空间，结合协变的泊松括号加倍结构及世界线上的算子乘积，推导场方程。

products on the ambitwistor worldlines. A conjecture arises that the kinematic

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: The interplay between string theory and early-universe cosmology offers

### [131] [Analytic Marginalization over Binary Variables in Physics Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.21912)
*Marcus Högås,Edvard Mörtsell*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种处理数据中二元效应的精确方法，其数学形式等同于统计物理中的伊辛模型，从而可以利用伊辛模型的工具进行快速准确的似然计算，并通过高效近似方案展示了在Ia型超新星校准等应用中的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 忽略数据测量中的二元效应（如属于两个群体之一或是否被污染）可能导致结果偏差，而显式建模这些效应因参数数量指数增长而难以实现。因此需要一种高效且精确的方法来处理这类问题。

Method: 通过建立二元修正的精确处理模型，发现其在一般条件下可转化为伊辛模型的形式，并利用伊辛模型的理论和算法工具进行高效似然计算，同时提出了低计算成本的近似方案。

Result: 实现了对包含二元效应的数据的快速准确分析，在Ia型超新星校准应用中表明宿主星系质量分类的不确定性对哈勃常数推断的影响可忽略。

Conclusion: 将二元效应问题映射到伊辛模型为处理此类高维参数问题提供了强大而高效的框架，具有广泛的应用潜力。

Abstract: In many data analyses, each measurement may come with a simple yes/no
correction; for example, belonging to one of two populations or being
contaminated or not. Ignoring such binary effects may bias the results, while
accounting for them explicitly quickly becomes infeasible as each of the $N$
data points introduces an additional parameter, resulting in an exponentially
growing number of possible configurations ($2^N$). We show that, under generic
conditions, an exact treatment of these binary corrections leads to a
mathematical form identical to the well-known Ising model from statistical
physics. This connection opens up a powerful set of tools developed for the
Ising model, enabling fast and accurate likelihood calculations. We present
efficient approximation schemes with minimal computational cost and demonstrate
their effectiveness in applications, including Type Ia supernova calibration,
where we show that the uncertainty in host-galaxy mass classification has
negligible impact on the inferred value of the Hubble constant.

</details>


### [132] [XRISM constraints on the velocity power spectrum in the Coma cluster](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.21918)
*D. Eckert,M. Markevitch,J. A. ZuHone,M. Regamey,I. Zhuravleva,Y. Ichinohe,N. Truong,N. Okabe,D. R. Wik*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 通过分析星系团内气体的速度场功率谱，理解物质的热化过程、AGN能量耗散及流体静力学假设的有效性。

Method: 采用基于模拟的推断方法，生成具有参数化功率谱模型的高斯随机场模拟，并前向建模观测效应（投影、发射加权、PSF模糊），训练神经网络以建立功率谱参数与观测数据之间的映射关系。

Result: 使用XRISM/Resolve两次指向即可准确测定湍流马赫数并对能量注入尺度施加约束；应用于Coma星系团得到注入尺度为2.2_{-1.0}^{+2.0} Mpc，积分至R500尺度下的三维马赫数为0.45_{-0.13}^{+0.18}，高于仅由速度弥散得出的值。

Abstract: The velocity field of intracluster gas in galaxy clusters contains key
information on the virialization of infalling material, the dissipation of AGN
energy into the surrounding medium, and the validity of the hydrostatic
hypothesis. The statistical properties of the velocity field are characterized
by its fluctuation power spectrum, which is usually expected to be well
described by an injection scale and a turbulent cascade. Here we propose a
simulation-based inference technique to retrieve the properties of the velocity
power spectrum from X-ray micro-calorimeter data by generating simulations of
Gaussian random fields from a parametric power spectrum model. We forward model
the measured bulk velocities and velocity dispersions by including the most
relevant observational effects (projection, emissivity weighting, PSF
smearing). We then train a neural network to learn the mapping between the
power spectrum parameters and the generated data vectors. Considering a
three-parameter model describing turbulent energy injection on large scales and
a power-law cascade, we found that two XRISM/Resolve pointings are sufficient
to accurately determine the turbulent Mach number and set interesting
constraints on the injection scale. Applying our method to the Coma cluster
data, we obtain a model that is characterized by a large injection scale that
rivals the size of the cluster ($\ell_{inj}=2.2_{-1.0}^{+2.0}$ Mpc). When this
power spectrum model is integrated over the cluster scales ($0<\ell<R_{500}=1.4
$Mpc), the Mach number of the gas motions is
$\mathcal{M}_{3D,500}=0.45_{-0.13}^{+0.18}$, which exceeds the value derived
from the velocity dispersions only. Further observations covering a wider area
are required to decrease the cosmic variance and constrain the slope of the
turbulent cascade.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 检测到最大尺度达521 kpc的纤维状弥散射电辐射，集成谱指数为-1.85±0.05，谱曲率为-0.93±0.21，且辐射形态与X射线ICM一致，呈现无序的谱指数分布。

poorly constrained due to the limited number of confirmed detections. This
study presents a detailed multi-frequency, high-sensitivity, and
high-resolution analysis of diffuse radio emission in the merging galaxy
cluster Abell 13. Using GMRT (147.5 MHz), uGMRT (400 MHz), ASKAP-low (887.5
MHz), and MGCLS (1284 MHz) images, we detect complex, filamentary diffuse

undergoing a merger, and the radio morphology reflects signatures of this
ongoing dynamical activity. We observed filamentary structures extending
towards east-northeast and southwest directions. The spectral index across the
emission appears irregular and lacks a coherent spatial gradient. The
integrated spectrum reveals a steep spectral index of -1.85 +/- 0.05 and a
spectral curvature of -0.93 +/- 0.21. These spectral properties, along with the
observed morphology and brightness distribution, are consistent with a
re-energization of a fossil radio plasma driven by adiabatic compression,
supporting the classification of the emission as a radio phoenix.
